Article

Publications from the Norwegian Mother, Father and Child Cohort Study

Published 17.07.2007 Updated 16.12.2022

The publications in the list below are based on data from the Norwegian Mother, Father and Child Cohort Study (MoBa).

The publications in the list below are based on data from the Norwegian Mother, Father and Child Cohort Study (MoBa).

You will find the most up-to-date publications list by searching for the Norwegian Mother and Child Cohort Study in PubMed.

NB! As of June 2019 the study includes "father" in its name, so please also search for Norwegian Mother, Father and Child Cohort Study in PubMed (for publications from June 2019 to today's date).

The list below is updated manually. Please inform us at when your articles are accepted for publication so that we can update the list.

Please use Ctrl+F and open all year banners to search the publication list.

As of December 1st 2022 a total of 1027 articles have been published based on MoBa.
